26  import java.nio.charset.Charset;
27  import java.nio.charset.CharsetDecoder;
28  import java.nio.charset.CharsetEncoder;
29  import sun.nio.cs.HistoricallyNamedCharset;
30  
31  public class EUC_CN_OLD
32      extends Charset
33      implements HistoricallyNamedCharset
34  {
35  
36      public EUC_CN_OLD() {
37          super("GB2312-OLD", null);
38      }
39  
40      public String historicalName() {
41          return "EUC_CN";
42      }
43  
44      public boolean contains(Charset cs) {
45          return ((cs instanceof EUC_CN_OLD)
46                  || (cs.name().equals("US-ASCII")));
47      }
48  
49      public CharsetDecoder newDecoder() {
50          return new Decoder(this);
51      }
52  
53      public CharsetEncoder newEncoder() {
54          return new Encoder(this);
55      }
56  
57      public short[] getDecoderIndex1() {
58          return Decoder.index1;
59      }
60      public String[] getDecoderIndex2() {
61          return Decoder.index2;
62      }
63      public short[] getEncoderIndex1() {
64          return Encoder.index1;
65      }
66      public String[] getEncoderIndex2() {
67          return Encoder.index2;
68      }
